Fanavard/classes/Sound.class.js

/**
 * Sound
 * @class Sound Manager - Main class to add and manage game sounds
 */
class Sound {

    /**
     * Play an audio from url
     * @param name
     * @return {Sound}
     */
    constructor (name){
        this.audio = new Audio('public/Mp3/' + name + '.mp3');
        return this;
    }


    /**
     * Plays the current instance of media
     * @return {Sound}
     */
    play(){
        if(this.audio) {
            this.audio.play();
        }
        return this;
    }

    /**
     * Pauses the current instance of media
     * @return {Sound}
     */
    pause(){
        if(this.audio) {
            this.audio.pause();
        }
        return this;
    }


    /**
     * Create instance correct name
     * @param key
     * @return {string}
     */
    static makeInstanceName(key){
        return key + "Instance";

    }


    /**
     * Make singleton design pattern to getv only one innstance of class.
     * @param key
     * @return {*}
     */
    static getInstance(key){
        let instanceName = Sound.makeInstanceName(key);
        return this[instanceName];
    }


    /**
     * Set instance
     * @param key
     * @param instance
     */
    static setInstance(key, instance){
        let instanceName = this.makeInstanceName(key);
        this[instanceName] = instance;
    }


    /**
     * Play sound based on it's name
     * @param key
     * @param canPlay
     */
    static playByKey(key , canPlay){

        if(!canPlay){
            return false;
        }

        const sounds = {
            loading:         let audioInstance;
        if(!(audioInstance = Sound.getInstance(key))) {
            audioInstance = new Audio(sounds[key]);
            Sound.setInstance(key , audioInstance);
        }

        audioInstance.play();
